           Comment by Eric Berthoumieux (2021-10-15):             2294000800006 
            The normalisation and sample thickness adjustment     2294000800007 
           were performed by adjusting the measured data on       2294000800008 
           ENDF/B-VI.8 below 0.1 eV and using the top of the 1st  2294000800009 
           resonance, that was close to saturation so has small   2294000800010 
           sensitivity to the sample thickness (a 10% change in   2294000800011 
           thickness gives a 2% change in yield close to the      2294000800012 
           resonance maximum), as shown in Fig.VII.10 p.160 of    2294000800013 
           Dirdi's thesis.                                        2294000800014
